CREATE TABLE SALES 
   (	ORDER_NUMBER VARCHAR(20), 
	PROD_CODE VARCHAR(20), 
	CUST_CODE VARCHAR(20), 
	SALE_DATE DATE, 
	CHANNEL_CODE VARCHAR(20), 
	PROMO_CODE VARCHAR(20), 
	QUANTITY_SOLD NUMERIC(10,2), 
	AMOUNT_SOLD NUMERIC(10,2), 
	INSERT_DT DATE, 
	LAST_UPDATE_DT DATE
   );
